        д  da tekkno hardcore bass-rythms... Thought about our ascii  д
        д  scene today... When I was getting into this great communi  д
        д  ty there were not so much wannabees & most of the beginne  д
        д  rs are now respected ascii artists. But nowadays many fin  д
        д  gs have changed... Wannabees atack our boards with theirs  д
        д  "1st collection"'s. They mostly suck and I don't know if   д
        д  any of them will reach our artistic level. Ok, there're a  д
        д  lso talented newcommers (like No Name/Bucket who is walki  д
        д  ng his own way of asciing) but I have an appeal to all of  д
        д  you - sysops, traders or whatever you are - PLEASE think   д
        д  for a while about your person as ascii artists. Not many   д
        д  of these wannabees will release more than 2 collies...     д

        д  more ascii artists loving the ascii scene & all this hell  д
        д  job like sitting for all days-long afront of CygnusEd (th  д
        д  anks, many thanks to the authors!!!)... We don't need the  д
        д  asciiers for one month... Think abt it!                    д
        д                                                             д

        д  ascii collies but rite now I left the scene. It's more im  д
        д  portant to be creative, active & friendly as hell. And be  д

        д  the reasons of being this scene so popular... A few month  д
        д  s ago I thought that it's cool 2 be called oldskool, but   д
        д  now I see what is the truth... Behemoth! You make clear    д

        д  RS OF NEWSCHOOL ASCII SCENE. And you, dear reader ?        д
